name:Y‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçw‚Äça‚Äçi‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçu‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçu
info:Hot Spring Room (Double Bed)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Couples
info:3 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted May 24, 2024
msg:A very satisfying stay~
The hotel is located in Huaqing Palace, and the decoration style is the same as that of Huaqing Palace. It feels like I live in Yang Guifei's home. The room has a small balcony, and you can see tourists when you look down, but as long as you draw the curtain, you will be isolated from the world. The private bath is very large, and it feels like there is no problem for four people to play mahjong. At 6:30 in the evening, the staff will come to add hot spring water and send goodnight soup, so as not to disturb the guests' rest at night, which is very considerate.
Dinner was at Yushanyuan, with rich dishes. The two-person meal purchased was cost-effective, and a vegetarian meal from Ci'en Temple was added, which tasted delicious and refreshing. The waiter was also very diligent. When he passed by and saw that the cup was not full, he would take the initiative to add tea. After dinner, you can ask the restaurant to arrange a pick-up and drop-off back to the room. Living here, you basically don't walk by yourself. It's so cool.
Let the hotel help book tickets for the Song of Everlasting Regret in advance. The location is almost in the middle of the middle A, and the experience is good. There are staff to lead the way before and after the performance, so you don't have to worry about getting lost in the dark, haha.
After watching the show, we returned to the room and the warm spring water was ready. We took the fruits and biscuits in the room and ate them while soaking. It was really super relaxing and relieved fatigue.
After the last performance of the Song of Everlasting Regret in the evening, there was basically no noise. It was also the time when the hot spring water supply ended. We could go to bed after washing. The bed was very large and comfortable. The pillow was soft and hard. It was not as good as at home, but I rarely had neck pain.
The next morning, I got up early and went to Yushanyuan for breakfast. There were many kinds of food, both Chinese and Western. The toast oven is worth praising. It was really the first time I had crispy toast for breakfast in a domestic hotel. If you want to do your job well, you must first sharpen your tools~
Then I strolled to Huaqing Palace. There were not many people in the morning, the weather was not hot, and it was very comfortable. After a stroll, there was a very beautiful garden and several bathtubs. The most attractive thing was the cultural and creative store.
After the stroll, I did the last thing, and went to the hotel's outdoor hot spring to soak in the hot spring! Our room was right next to the hot spring, which was very convenient to go there. Maybe it was a weekday so there weren't many people. There were only a few aunties soaking in the same pool with me. The staff took the initiative to ask what I needed to drink and provided free fruit. It felt like a vacation.
There were no disadvantages in the whole process. The only thing was that there were quite a few flies in the outdoor hot spring, and they were quite big üòÇ Other than that, there was nothing I was dissatisfied with üëçüèª

msg:The service from before check-in to during check-in was really a good experience, very smooth. Here I want to thank Butler Deng for helping us book tickets for the C position of Song of Everlasting Regret before check-in. After check-in, he learned that we were going to climb Huashan Mountain and specially recommended the appropriate path up and down the mountain. Even if it was not working hours, he responded attentively and helped to achieve various requests. The cleaning staff who assisted in cleaning during the stay were very careful. They found that we had the habit of making tea, and put an extra box of tissues for our convenience. Originally, we only booked to stay for 2 nights, but we liked it so much that we stayed for another night.
The hotel is part of the Huaqing Pool Scenic Area. Guests can enter and exit Huaqing Palace at any time with the hotel door card. During the 4 days we stayed, we chose to stay early in the morning and in the evening, imagining the prosperous scene of the Tang Dynasty, and wandering around the palace. The Huaqing Palace without the noise of tourists is another kind of beauty. Love it!
At night, the hotel butler carried the ancient dragon head lantern and led the guests to appreciate Song of Everlasting Regret, which was unique.
During the stay, we soaked in the hot springs that were the same as those thousands of years ago. The water was smooth and moist, and paired with the pear and tremella soup specially made by the hotel, it was another kind of happiness.
Huaqing Yutang Hotel gave us a very different and unique experience on this trip. This trip went all the way from Hangzhou to Xi'an, and we stayed in many international chain hotels and luxury hotels. I think Huaqing Yutang can be compared with international luxury hotels. We will definitely visit again

There is a tour guide explaining it when we walk to the front door. I didn't do any strategy before coming here, and I thought it was just a few hot spring pools. But the children listened with relish to the tour guide's explanation. After telling the story of Yang Guifei, I thought the tour was over, but I didn't expect that after a few turns, I came to the place where the Xi'an Incident took place. It turned out that Chiang Kai-shek lived in Huaqing Palace when he came to Xi'an. We all know this history, and it is still shocking to see the old site.
After the visit, we had dinner at Yushanyuan. The products are average, not particularly outstanding.
It is highly recommended to watch the Song of Everlasting Regret in Huaqing Palace at night. We first gathered in the hotel lobby, and the staff would light the palace lanterns to take us there, which was very interesting.
After watching the performance, we returned to the room to soak in the hot spring. The waiter also gave us Tremella soup. The waiter of the hot spring pool in the room came to help us drain the water at 7 o'clock, and the water has been circulating since then. Because I heard the story of Yang Guifei in the afternoon, I was particularly happy when I took a hot spring bath at nightüòä
After breakfast the next day, I went to the Terracotta Warriors, which was not far away.
In less than a day at the hotel, I experienced everything I wanted to do and see, which was very relaxing and comfortable. The hotel is very clean, and the service of the front desk and room attendants is very enthusiastic. I really feel at home.
The only regret is that if the dinner and breakfast of Yushanyuan can be improved, it will be perfect.
